    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">Tomorrow is Programmers’ Day! 🎉 And it made us remember how once upon a time, every bug fix was celebrated with this rubber chicken’s scream in the office. Now we’re remote, coding from everywhere, but our spirit is the same: still one team, one heartbeat. 🫶 Happy Programmers’ Day no matter how far away! <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fatolye15&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#atolye15</a></p>
